# Jonas Hallstrom, 2022
# Notes:
# - %_Ito and Vol_Ito are based on roughly how much of the body matter had maximum temperatures between 1073 and 1273 K
## But they are not fully representative of the requirements to match the parent body material, just a quick guide/approximation
# - The tempK_enter_exit columns give the two times at which the body's core entered and exited that temperature, in seconds, where -1 means never entered or exited.
# - Note that kappa and cp multi are actual multipliers, e.g. multiplying by 1.1, whereas the corresponding number to be entered into the simulation code would be the percentage, e.g. 110
